\x65\x61\x6D\x73\x3C\x2F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3E\x3C\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x3D\x22\x3A\x65\x78\x70\x65\x72\x69\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x61\x6C\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x69\x74\x72\x3D\x22\x67\x61\x6D\x65\x6D\x6F\x64\x65\x5F\x65\x78\x70\x65\x72\x69\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x61\x6C\x22\x3E\x45\x78\x70\x65\x72\x69\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x61\x6C\x3C\x2F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3E\x3C\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x3D\x22\x3A\x70\x61\x72\x74\x79\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x69\x74\x72\x3D\x22\x70\x61\x72\x74\x79\x22\x3E\x50\x61\x72\x74\x79\x3C\x2F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3E\x3C\x2F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x69\x64\x3D\x22\x6C\x6F\x63\x61\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x4B\x6E\x6F\x77\x6E\x22\x3E\x3C\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x20\x69\x64\x3D\x22\x72\x65\x67\x69\x6F\x6E\x22\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x66\x6F\x72\x6D\x2D\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x72\x6F\x6C\x22\x20\x6F\x6E\x63\x68\x61\x6E\x67\x65\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x74\x52\x65\x67\x69\x6F\x6E\x28\x24\x28\x27\x23\x72\x65\x67\x69\x6F\x6E\x27\x29\x2E\x76\x61\x6C\x28\x29\x29\x22\x20\x72\x65\x71\x75\x69\x72\x65\x64\x3D\x22\x22\x3E\x3C\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x65\x64\x22\x20\x64\x69\x73\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x64\x3D\x22\x64\x69\x73\x61\x62\x6C\x65\x64\x22\x20\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x3D\x22\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x69\x74\x72\x3D\x22\x72\x65\x67\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x73\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x22\x3E\x2D\x2D\x20\x53\x65\x6C\x65\x63\x74\x20\x61\x20\x52\x65\x67\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x2D\x2D\x3C\x2F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3E\x3C\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x3D\x22\x55\x53\x2D\x41\x74\x6C\x61\x6E\x74\x61\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x69\x74\x72\x3D\x22\x72\x65\x67\x69\x6F\x6E\x5F\x6E\x6F\x72\x74\x68\x5F\x61\x6D\x65\x72\x69\x63\x61\x22\x3E\x4E\x6F\x72\x74\x68\x20\x41\x6D\x65\x72\x69\x63\x61\x3C\x2F\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x3E\x3C\x6F\x70\x74\x69\x6F\x6E\x20\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x3D\x22\x42\x52\x2D\x42\x72\x61\x7A\x69\x6C\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74 \x3E\x3C\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x20\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x73\x75\x62\x6D\x69\x74\x22\x20\x6F\x6E\x63\x6C\x69\x63\x6B\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x74\x4E\x69\x63\x6B\x28\x64\x6F\x63\x75\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x2E\x67\x65\x74\x45\x6C\x65\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x42\x79\x49\x64\x28\x27\x6E\x69\x63\x6B\x27\x29\x2E\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x29\x3B\x20\x72\x65\x74\x75\x72\x6E\x20\x66\x61\x6C\x73\x65\x22\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x62\x74\x6E\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x70\x6C\x61\x79\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x70\x72\x69\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x6E\x65\x65\x64\x73\x2D\x73\x65\x72\x76\x65\x72\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x69\x74\x72\x3D\x22\x70\x6C\x61\x79\x22\x3E\x50\x6C\x61\x79\x3C\x2F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3E\x20\x3C\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x20\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x73\x75\x62\x6D\x69\x74\x22\x20\x6F\x6E\x63\x6C\x69\x63\x6B\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x74\x4E\x69\x63\x6B\x28\x64\x6F\x63\x75\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x2E\x67\x65\x74\x45\x6C\x65\x6D\x65\x6E\x74\x42\x79\x49\x64\x28\x27\x6E\x69\x63\x6B\x27\x29\x2E\x76\x61\x6C\x75\x65\x29\x3B\x20\x72\x65\x74\x75\x72\x6E\x20\x66\x61\x6C\x73\x65\x22\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x62\x74\x6E\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x70\x6C\x61\x79\x2D\x67\x75\x65\x73\x74\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x73\x75\x63\x63\x65\x73\x73\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x6E\x65\x65\x64\x73\x2D\x73\x65\x72\x76\x65\x72\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x69\x74\x72\x3D\x22\x70\x6C\x61\x79\x5F\x61\x73\x5F\x67\x75\x65\x73\x74\x22\x3E\x50\x6C\x61\x79\x20\x61\x73\x20\x67\x75\x65\x73\x74\x3C\x2F\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x3E\x20\x3C\x62\x75\x74\x74\x6F\x6E\x20\x6F\x6E\x63\x6C\x69\x63\x6B\x3D\x22\x72\x65\x74\x75\x72\x6E\x20\x66\x61\x63\x65\x62\x6F\x6F\x6B\x4C\x6F\x67\x69\x6E\x28\x29\x2C\x21\x31\x22\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x62\x74\x6E\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x6C\x6F\x67\x69\x6E\x20\x62\x74\x6E\x2D\x70\x72\x69\x6D\x61\x72\x79\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x6F\x72\x69\x67\x69\x6E\x61\x6C\x2D\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x3D\x22\x22\x20\x74\x69\x74\x6C\x65\x3D\x22\x22\x3E\x3C\x73\x70\x61\x6E\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x69\x74\x72\x3D\x22\x6C\x6F\x67 \x6F\x74\x3D\x22\x32\x33\x38\x33\x31\x34\x32\x33\x31\x35\x22\x20\x64\x61\x74\x61\x2D\x61\x64\x2D\x66\x6F\x72\x6D\x61\x74\x3D\x22\x72\x65\x63\x74\x61\x6E\x67\x6C\x65\x22\x3E\x3C\x2F\x69\x6E\x73\x3E\x3C\x73\x63\x72\x69\x70\x74\x3E\x28\x61\x64\x73\x62\x79\x67\x6F\x6F\x67\x6C\x65\x3D\x77\x69\x6E\x64\x6F\x77\x2E\x61\x64\x73\x62\x79\x67\x6F\x6F\x67\x6C\x65\x7C\x7C\x5B\x5D\x29\x2E\x70\x75\x73\x68\x28\x7B\x7D\x29\x3C\x2F\x73\x63\x72\x69\x70\x74\x3E\x3C\x2F\x63\x65\x6E\x74\x65\x72\x3E\x3C\x2F\x64\x69\x76\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x72\x6F\x6C\x65\x3D\x22\x74\x61\x62\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x22\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x74\x61\x62\x2D\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x20\x66\x61\x64\x65\x22\x20\x69\x64\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x22\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x7A\x6F\x6F\x6D\x53\x70\x65\x65\x64\x22\x3E\x3C\x2F\x64\x69\x76\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6E\x74\x61\x69\x6E\x65\x72\x22\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x73\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x52\x6F\x77\x22\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x2D\x78\x73\x2D\x36\x20\x66\x69\x72\x73\x74\x53\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x22\x3E\x3C\x2F\x64\x69\x76\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x63\x6F\x6C\x2D\x78\x73\x2D\x36\x20\x73\x65\x63\x6F\x6E\x64\x53\x65\x74\x74\x69\x6E\x67\x73\x22\x3E\x3C\x2F\x64\x69\x76\x3E\x3C\x2F\x64\x69\x76\x3E\x3C\x2F\x64\x69\x76\x3E\x3C\x2F\x64\x69\x76\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x72\x6F\x6C\x65\x3D\x22\x74\x61\x62\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x6C\x22\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x74\x61\x62\x2D\x70\x61\x6E\x65\x20\x66\x61\x64\x65\x22\x20\x69\x64\x3D\x22\x74\x68\x65\x6D\x69\x6E\x67\x22\x3E\x3C\x64\x69\x76\x20\x63\x6C\x61\x73\x73\x3D\x22\x66\x6F\x72\x6D\x2D\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x70\x22\x3E\x3C\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x3E\x42\x61\x63\x6B\x67\x72\x6F\x75\x6E\x64\x20\x43\x6F\x6C\x6F\x72\x3C\x2F\x6C\x61\x62\x65\x6C\x3E\x3C\x69\x6E\x70\x75\x74\x20\x74\x79\x70\x65\x3D\x22\x74\x65\x78\x74\x22\x20\x69\x64\x3D\x22\x62\x61\x63
